<a id="27809" href="Frame.html#27744" class="Function">frame-is-univ-str</a> <a id="27827" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27829" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#2442" class="Function">SNS‚ÜíUnivalentStr</a> <a id="27846" href="Frame.html#25215" class="Function">isHomoEqv</a> <a id="27856" href="Frame.html#27302" class="Function">frame-is-SNS</a>

<a id="27870" class="Comment">-- Similar to the poset case, this is sufficient to establish that the category of frames</a>
<a id="27960" class="Comment">-- is univalent</a>

<a id="‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°"></a><a id="27977" href="Frame.html#27977" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="27982" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27984" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27985" href="Frame.html#27985" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="27987" href="Frame.html#27987" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="27989" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27991" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="27997" href="Basis.html#2446" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="28000" href="Basis.html#2449" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="28003" href="Basis.html#2452" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÇ</a><a id="28005" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28007" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="28009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28010" href="Frame.html#27985" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="28012" href="Frame.html#25455" class="Function Operator">‚âÉf</a> <a id="28015" href="Frame.html#27987" class="Bound">G</a><a id="28016" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28018" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Glue.html#1051" class="Function Operator">‚âÉ</a> <a id="28020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28021" href="Frame.html#27985" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="28023" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="28025" href="Frame.html#27987" class="Bound">G</a><a id="28026" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="28028" href="Frame.html#27977" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="28033" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28035" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#4416" class="Function">SIP</a> <a id="28039" href="Frame.html#27744" class="Function">frame-is-univ-str</a>

<a id="28058" class="Comment">-- However, there are two minor issues with this.</a>
<a id="28108" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28111" class="Comment">--   1. We do not have to talk about equivalences as we are talking about sets;</a>
<a id="28191" class="Comment">--      isomorphisms are well-behaved in our case as we are dealing with sets.</a>
<a id="28270" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28273" class="Comment">--  2. We do not have to require the frame data to be preserved. We can show that any</a>
<a id="28359" class="Comment">--     poset isomorphism preserves the frame operators.</a>
<a id="28415" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28418" class="Comment">-- We will therefore strengthen our result to work with the notion of poset isomorphism.</a>

<a id="28508" class="Comment">-- We start by showing the equivalence between ‚âÉf and ‚âÖ‚Çö.</a>

<a id="34009" class="Comment">-- Now that we have this result, we can move on to show that given two frames F and G,</a>
<a id="34096" class="Comment">-- (pos F) ‚âÖ‚Çö (pos G) is equivalent to F ‚â° G.</a>
